aristocratos: Rust Plugin: Large Oil Refinery  The Large Oil Refinery is an advanced crafting and production system for Rust, designed as a late-game item requiring significant investment.    ### Main Features:   - Multiple Slots:     - 2‚Äì3 Input slots for materials (e.g., high-quality metal, low-grade fuel).     - 3‚Äì4 Output slots for refined products (e.g., diesel).   - Can use two fuel types simultaneously (e.g., wood and crude oil).   - Diesel Production:     - Consumes 10 units of high-quality metal & low-grade fuel.     - Requires large amounts of crude oil.   - Configurable Settings:     - Adjustable processing times, resource requirements, upgrade costs, and recipe outputs.     - Spawn rate and locations in loot boxes or airdrops can be customized.    ---  ### Improved UI System:   - User-friendly interface with three sections:     - Inventory (input/output slots)     - Upgrade panel     - Recipe selection   - Interactive Features:     - Drag & Drop functionality     - Status indicators for active processes    ---  ### Upgrade System:   - Three upgrade categories:     1. Speed: Up to 60% faster production     2. Efficiency: Up to 45% less fuel consumption     3. Output: Up to 50% more production   - Maximum upgrade levels per category, increasing costs per level    ---  ### Effects & Sounds:   - Dynamic fire effect system   - Smoke particles based on activity   - Realistic processing sounds & visual feedback for upgrades    ---  ### Expanded Recipes:   - Includes all functions of the small refinery:     - Crude Oil ‚Üí Low Grade Fuel     - Animal Fat ‚Üí Low Grade Fuel   - New recipes:     - Diesel production     - High-efficiency fuel processing    ---  ### Workbench Level 3 Requirement:   - Can only be crafted at a Workbench Level 3.   - Must be researched before use.   - Usage requires a Workbench Level 3 within a 5-meter radius.    ### Additional Security Measures:   - Workbench proximity is checked during every processing cycle.   - Player receives a notification if no Workbench Level 3 is nearby.   - Usage is blocked without a proper workbench.    The Large Oil Refinery is a late-game item that requires significant investment:   - 1 Workbench Level 3 must be built.   - The blueprint must be researched.   - High material costs for crafting. Designs are included.

LAGZYA: using Oxide.Core.Plugins; using Oxide.Core; using System.Collections.Generic; using Network;  namespace Oxide.Plugins {     [Info("Server Balancer", "Author", "1.0.0")]     [Description("–ë–∞–ª–∞–Ω—Å–∏—Ä–æ–≤—â–∏–∫ –Ω–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∏ –º–µ–∂–¥—É —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞–º–∏ Rust")]     class ServerBalancer : RustPlugin     {         private Configuration config;         private int currentIndex = 0;          private class Configuration         {             public List<string> Servers { get; set; } = new List<string>             {                 "192.168.1.10:28015",                 "192.168.1.11:28015"             };         }          protected override void LoadDefaultConfig() => config = new Configuration();         protected override void LoadConfig()         {             base.LoadConfig();             config = Config.ReadObject<Configuration>();         }          void Init()         {             LoadConfig();             SaveConfig();         }          object OnPlayerPreAuth(Connection connection, string ip)         {             if (config.Servers.Count == 0) return null;              // –í—ã–±–æ—Ä —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞ –ø–æ round-robin             var targetServer = config.Servers[currentIndex];             currentIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % config.Servers.Count;              // –ü–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Å–æ–µ–¥–∏–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è             RedirectPlayer(connection, targetServer);                          // –ë–ª–æ–∫–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –ø–æ–¥–∫–ª—é—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∫ —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–º—É —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä—É             return true;         }          private void RedirectPlayer(Connection connection, string target)         {             var player = connection.player as BasePlayer;             if (player == null) return;              // –û—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∫–∞ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥—ã –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–¥–∫–ª—é—á–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫ —Ü–µ–ª–µ–≤–æ–º—É —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä—É             player.SendConsoleCommand("client.connect", target);
